# CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED

### Leave site?

You're about to leave our website and go to an external link. Are you sure?

Capsitech It Services Private Limited, is an unlisted private company incorporated on 16 August, 2014. It is classified as a private limited company and is located in , Rajasthan. It's authorized share capital is INR 9.00 lac and the total paid-up capital is INR 2.00 lac.  
  
Capsitech It Services's operating revenue range is INR 1 cr - 100 cr for the financial year ending on 31 March, 2024. It's EBITDA has increased by 61.63% over the previous year. At the same time, it's book networth has increased by 78.84%.

The current status of Capsitech It Services Private Limited is - Active.  
  
The last reported AGM (Annual General Meeting) of Capsitech It Services Private Limited, per our records, was held on 30 September, 2024.   
  
The company has 4 directors - Mohit Baheti, Satya Narayan Jangid, and others.  
  
The Corporate Identification Number (CIN) of Capsitech It Services Private Limited is U72900RJ2014PTC046083. It's registered address is at H 298-299 3RD PHASE RIICO INDUSTRIAL AREA BORANADA, ,BORANADA, Jodhpur, JODHPUR, Rajasthan, India, 342012, - 342012.

## About us

Capsitech IT Services is a fintech and technology innovation company, building scalable digital platforms for modern businesses. We develop enterprise software, fintech solutions, cloud platforms, and intelligent automation systems that help organizations operate faster, smarter, and more securely. From custom software development to full-scale digital ecosystems, we partner with businesses to transform ideas into powerful technology products that drive measurable growth. Innovation. Scalability. Digital Transformation.

## About CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED

CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED is a Private Limited Company and was incorporated on Aug 16, 2014 in India.It is registered at Registrar of Companies, ROC Jaipur.Its registered address is H 298-299 3RD PHASE RIICO INDUSTRIAL AREA BORANADA, ,BORANADA, Jodhpur, JODHPUR, Rajasthan, India, 342012. Its corporate identification number is (CIN) U72900RJ2014PTC046083 and its current status is Active.Its industry classification as per MCA is other Computer Related Activities [For Example Maintenance Of Websites Of Other Firms/ Creation Of Multimedia Presentations For Other Firms Etc.].It had a team size of 374 employees as on Aug 31, 2025.

CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED's last Annual General Meeting (AGM) was held on Sep 30, 2024 as per records from Ministry of Corporate Affairs (MCA).CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED's authorised share capital is Rs. 900,000 and its paid up capital is Rs. 200,000.

CAPSITECH IT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED generated a revenue of Rs. 37.4Cr for the financial year ending on Mar 31, 2025.

# Chairman's Address

### As we embark on a new academic year,

Capsitech Institute of Technology stands as a beacon of excellence in imparting industry-oriented technical training to students. Our commitment to providing advanced knowledge, innovative skills, and a strong ethical foundation ensures the development of leaders in the ever-evolving landscape of technology. Our students are trained by industry leaders who actively work on several international projects, emphasising experiential learning and the practical implementation of theoretical concepts.

At Capsitech, we provide students with unparalleled opportunities to engage in live projects that enhance their exposure to real-world problem-solving experiences. Our state-of-the-art laboratories and research facilities contribute to today's dynamic market, enhancing the thinking skills, adaptability, and innovative spirit of our students.

Our diverse inclusion of students enriches the fabric of our Institute's community and fosters a culture of mutual respect and understanding. With an outstanding environment that promotes learning and placements, our students get a chance to work with professionals and earn an initial starting package of 12 lacs per annum.

As we commence this exciting journey together, let us uphold the values that define our institute and inspire us to commit ourselves to making a positive impact in the world. Join us at Capsitech Institute of Technology and seize the opportunity to become a leader in the field of technology.

Dave Jangid

 Chairman

# Empowering Innovation,

 Driving Excellence

Founded in the year 2014, Capsitech IT Services is one of the leading fintech companies in the city of Jodhpur, Rajasthan. The company offers a wide range of services through technical tools that are developed to ease the lives of customers and clients. From the world of accounting to the retail industry, the team at Capsitech has marked its presence in several sectors propelling the use of digital alternatives for faster, better, and pocket-friendly solutions.

We invest in the ideas that can mitigate the existing problems in businesses and bridge the gap between demand and supply by creating the technical solutions that befit the requirements of the businesses.

# Technical Proficiency

Our team has mastery in comprehending the business challenges and then develop ideal solutions to ameliorate the business process by placing the technical platform as a medium of increasing the productivity of the businesses processes.

The technical team at Capsitech is skilled to develop technical tools and mobile applications by using the latest technologies available. # Research and Development

Our research and development wing makes attempts to examine the business processes and then identify the existing problems or sections that requires an added technical support for better functioning.

We, at Capsitech, understand the significance of focusing on meticulous details of a business before developing a solution for it and hence, a copious amount of importance is given to the research wing.

In the course of the development of our products, the results and the analysis made during the research phase plays the biggest role in determining the development strategies for the technical team.

## Frequently Asked Questions about CAPSITECH LIMITED

Detailed answers about CAPSITECH LIMITED, including incorporation, status, business activity, and accounts information.

When was CAPSITECH LIMITED founded? 

CAPSITECH LIMITED was officially incorporated on 09 April 2013 and is registered under company number 08479483. Incorporation establishes the company as a legal entity registered at Companies House, allowing it to trade, enter contracts, and operate under UK company law.

What type of company is CAPSITECH LIMITED? 

Private limited with Share Capital. This classification indicates the legal structure of the company, which determines the way it is governed, its liability, and regulatory obligations. For example, a private limited company (Ltd) limits the personal liability of its shareholders.

What is the current status of CAPSITECH LIMITED? 

CAPSITECH LIMITED's current status is Active. The company status indicates whether it is actively trading, dormant, or has been dissolved. Maintaining an active status is essential for legally conducting business, filing accounts, and maintaining credibility with partners and lenders.

What does CAPSITECH LIMITED do? 

CAPSITECH LIMITED operates in the following sector: 62012 Business and domestic software development - Business and domestic software development . This provides insight into the company’s primary business activities and industry focus. Knowing the SIC code and description is useful for market research, assessing competitors, and understanding potential business risks.

What is CAPSITECH LIMITED's registered address? 

The registered office address of CAPSITECH LIMITED is Flat 10 Heath House, Main Road, Sidcup, Kent, DA14 6NJ. This is the official address filed with Companies House for legal and statutory correspondence.

Is CAPSITECH LIMITED financially stable? 

Based on the latest accounts up to 16 Sep 2024, CAPSITECH LIMITED has filed financial statements showing its assets, liabilities, and overall trading performance. The next accounts are due by 30 Sep 2025. Reviewing these accounts helps assess the company’s financial stability, creditworthiness, and risk profile, which is crucial for investors, suppliers, and potential business partners.

# Future Prospects

Anticipating the Business Needs

We strive to assimilate the needs the business may face in the future, and we intend to develop and effectuate next-generation solutions that may potentially ensure the smooth progression of the business trajectory. Our expertise lies in comprehending the challenges that are faced by businesses of varied domains and developing potential, futuristic solutions.

Our aspirations of excelling as a one-stop solution to your business requirements are premised upon the idea of ensuring comprehensive growth and development of complementary businesses in different sectors.

#### Product Development

We excel in the creation of cloud-based technical solutions that are developed with strong research and efficacious implementation of the well-planned strategies that can meet the requirements of the clients and customers.

#### Talent Outsourcing

We serve the suffering businesses by providing them with sectional services to overcome the challenges, establish rewarding operational modules, and augment the pace of seamless progression.

#### Training

We invite applications from aspiring professionals who are willing to enhance their practical knowledge and develop their careers in the industry. Our training modules are designed to upskill the aspirants on the practical front.

# Working

 Mechanism

We have a number of successful organizations under our belt that are comprehensively designed and developed by our skilled team. Our working methodologies encompass the integration of sectional development and extensive planning. Our working protocols include, but are not limited to, the following stages of development:

Making proactive research to understand the market demands.
Identifying the project's potential, loopholes, associated risks, and development modules.
Consultations between the teams and finalizing the plan of execution.
Allocating the responsibilities to the team members and assigning individual goals.
Initiating the ideation process and working towards the Minimum Viable Product.
Making relentless attempts to ensure the development of a successful business.

About Capsitech Institute Of Technology Private Limited

**Capsitech Institute Of Technology Private Limited**, a active private limited company, was established on 29 December 2015 in Boranada, Rajasthan, India. Engaging in software within the printing & publishing sector, it holds CIN: U85499RJ2015PTC048950. Registered under ROC Roc Jaipur. it is unlisted. It has an authorized capital of ₹0.10 M and a paid-up capital of ₹0.10 M.

It upholds a compliant status. Its leadership includes [Sukhdeo Jangid](https://www.thecompanycheck.com/people-profile/sukhdeo-jangid/06410764) (Director), [Satya Narayan Jangid](https://www.thecompanycheck.com/people-profile/satya-narayan-jangid/06410763) (Director). Its latest AGM occurred on 30 September 2025, with the balance sheet filed on 31 March 2025. It is based at H 298-299, 3Rd Phase Riico Industrial Area, Boranada, Rajasthan, 342012.

# Dave Jangid

### CEO & Founder

Contact

Dave Jangid is the CEO and Founder of Debitam, offering online account filing services for small businesses in the UK. With a background in IT and accounting, he has also founded Capsitech Limited and Capium Limited, specializing in IT projects and online accounting software. Prior to his entrepreneurial ventures, Dave worked as an Account Manager at McMillan Woods, where he handled financial advice for corporate clients. He holds a Master's degree in Business Administration from the University of London and a Bachelor's degree in Business Administration from Jai Narain Vyas University.

Location

London, United Kingdom

## Privacy Preference Center

When you visit any website, it may store or retrieve information on your browser, mostly in the form of cookies. This information might be about you, your preferences or your device and is mostly used to make the site work as you expect it to. The information does not usually directly identify you, but it can give you a more personalized web experience. Because we respect your right to privacy, you can choose not to allow some types of cookies. Click on the different category headings to find out more and change our default settings. However, blocking some types of cookies may impact your experience of the site and the services we are able to offer. 

[More information](https://cookiepedia.co.uk/giving-consent-to-cookies)

Allow All
### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Performance Cookies

- [x] Performance Cookies 

These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### Functional Cookies

- [x] Functional Cookies 

These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.

#### Targeting Cookies

- [x] Targeting Cookies 

These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## About CAPSITECH INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY PRIVATE LIMITED

CAPSITECH INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY PRIVATE LIMITED is a Private Limited Company and was incorporated on Dec 29, 2015 in India.It is registered at Registrar of Companies, ROC Jaipur.Its registered address is H 298-299, 3RD PHASE RIICO INDUSTRIAL AREA, Jodhpur, BORANADA, Rajasthan, India, 342012. Its corporate identification number is (CIN) U85499RJ2015PTC048950 and its current status is Active.Its industry classification as per MCA is other Educational Services N.e.c.

CAPSITECH INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY PRIVATE LIMITED's last Annual General Meeting (AGM) was held on Sep 30, 2024 as per records from Ministry of Corporate Affairs (MCA).CAPSITECH INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY PRIVATE LIMITED's authorised share capital is Rs. 100,000 and its paid up capital is Rs. 100,000.

CAPSITECH INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY PRIVATE LIMITED generated a revenue of Rs. 54.4L for the financial year ending on Mar 31, 2025.

## Overview

Capsitech is a technology-focused company operating in the IT and consulting sectors, with locations in the United Kingdom and India. Founded in 2013 and renamed in 2014, the company specializes in providing a wide range of technology, consulting, and outsourcing solutions aimed at facilitating digital transformation for businesses.

The services offered include technology consulting, software development, web design and development, outsourcing solutions, research and development, and training. The company develops cloud-based solutions, mobile applications, and custom software platforms that enhance productivity and streamline business processes. Capsitech serves a diverse clientele, supporting startups and established businesses in overcoming operational challenges and exploring new market opportunities. The leadership team guides the company in delivering innovative and effective solutions tailored to meet the needs of its clients, maintaining a commitment to ethical practices and strong client relationships.

* [Aman Singh](https://in.linkedin.com/in/aman-singh-92785b1b2?trk=public_post_feed-actor-name)

  + [Report this post](/uas/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fposts%2Faman-singh-92785b1b2_hpcl-grouptask-gtpreparation-activity-7379040297567186944-uqLN&trk=public_post_ellipsis-menu-semaphore-sign-in-redirect&guestReportContentType=POST&_f=guest-reporting)

  ✅ How to Tackle the HPCL Group Task (GT) – My Experience & Tips Last Year, I appeared for the HPCL Group Task (GT) and wanted to share my learnings to help future aspirants prepare the right way. 📄 Format of the GT (in my case) • You are given a business case (150–200 words) printed on an A4 sheet. • 5 minutes to read and understand it. • Then, each candidate presents their analysis and proposed solutions. 📌 My Case Topic (Summary): A company operates in Steel and Textile sectors. The textile side has great fabric products, and the steel side has strong leadership. The company wants to expand both globally while ensuring: • No employee overburdening • Work-life balance • Proper budget allocation • Equal focus on marketing & manufacturing • Growth opportunities for lower executives 💡 My Key Suggestions in the GT: 1. Since good fabrics are already available, we can avoid spending heavily on R&D in textiles. It’s important to know where not to spend, not just where to invest. 2. For steel, since we know about resources like hematite and magnetite, we can set up or expand manufacturing units near those geographical locations to reduce costs and boost efficiency. 3. Encourage hiring of freshers – their fresh perspectives and ideas can drive innovation and energy into the system. 4. Skill-based work allocation will lead to better productivity and avoid employee burnout. 5. Give employees space and flexibility to come up with their own solutions – this builds ownership and motivation. 🎯 Tips to Clear HPCL GT: • Read fast, identify core problems, and stay structured. • Address every constraint/requirement in the case. • Keep your ideas practical and business-oriented, not just idealistic. • Maintain clarity, confidence, and brevity while speaking. 📬 Feel free to reach out if you’re preparing for PSU interviews – happy to help. # 23 Biggest Technology Acquisitions in 2024

By [Blake Hutchison](https://flippa.com/blog/author/blake-hutchison/)

Updated: Apr 24, 2025

![Facebook](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%2024%2024'%3E%3C/svg%3E "Facebook")

The year 2024 saw a surge in major technology acquisitions as companies pursued strategic buyouts to strengthen their artificial intelligence, cloud computing, and cybersecurity positions. This trend reflected the tech industry’s push for innovation, market dominance, and operational efficiency.

With growing competition and rapid advancements, businesses aimed to acquire specialized technologies and talent pools. AI-driven companies, cloud providers, and cybersecurity firms were at the forefront of these deals, signaling a shift toward consolidation and vertical integration.

These high-profile acquisitions not only reshaped the competitive landscape but also demonstrated how companies are leveraging M&A strategies to drive digital transformation, optimize infrastructure, and enhance security measures.

## Major Technology Acquisitions in 2024

The technology sector experienced a wave of high-profile acquisitions in 2024, with companies [strategically merging or acquiring competitors](https://flippa.com/blog/tech-ma-trends-report-2025/) to expand their capabilities in artificial intelligence, cloud computing, and cybersecurity. These deals ranged from multi-billion-dollar takeovers to targeted acquisitions to enhance technological expertise and market reach.

AI-driven automation, data security, and cloud infrastructure were key focus areas, as businesses sought to strengthen their offerings in response to increasing demand for advanced digital solutions. This period of consolidation reflected a broader trend of companies positioning themselves for long-term growth by integrating cutting-edge technologies and top-tier talent.

Below are some of the biggest technology acquisitions of the year, each playing a significant role in shaping the competitive landscape:

### Xerox Bought Lexmark for $1.5 Billion

Xerox expanded its presence in the office printing and enterprise solutions market by acquiring Lexmark in a $1.5 billion deal. This move strengthened Xerox’s managed print services, integrating Lexmark’s hardware and software capabilities into its portfolio.

* The acquisition was valued at $1.5 billion, including net debt and other assumed liabilities.
* Lexmark, headquartered in Lexington, Kentucky, is a global leader in business imaging and printing solutions.
* Xerox aimed to enhance its document management services and improve efficiency in enterprise printing.
* The deal allowed Xerox to expand its customer base and strengthen its position in the print technology sector.

### Cisco Bought Splunk for $28 Billion

Cisco made a major move in cybersecurity and AI-powered data analytics [by acquiring Splunk for $28 billion](https://www.wsj.com/articles/cisco-closes-28-billion-acquisition-of-splunk-betting-big-on-ai-836b6560). This acquisition positioned Cisco as a real-time threat detection and security automation leader.

* The deal was valued at $28 billion in an all-cash transaction, with Cisco paying $157 per share.
* Splunk specializes in data analytics and cybersecurity, helping businesses analyze, monitor, and protect their IT environments.
* Cisco integrated Splunk’s technology into its broader security portfolio to enhance real-time threat detection.
* The acquisition reinforced Cisco’s transition into AI-powered security and observability solutions.

### IBM Purchased HashiCorp for $6.4 Billion

IBM expanded its cloud automation capabilities by acquiring HashiCorp for $6.4 billion. The deal aimed to strengthen IBM’s hybrid cloud offerings and improve enterprise infrastructure automation.

* IBM announced the acquisition in early 2024, planning full integration by year-end.
* HashiCorp is known for its infrastructure automation tools, including Terraform, Vault, and Consul, which are widely used in cloud computing.
* The acquisition enabled IBM to provide enterprises with advanced cloud security, automation, and management tools.
* HashiCorp’s software complemented IBM’s AI-driven cloud infrastructure services, making deployments more scalable and secure.

### SAP Acquired WalkMe for $1.5 Billion

* WalkMe is a leading digital adoption platform that simplifies enterprise software use through automation and guided workflows.
* SAP integrated WalkMe into its Joule AI-powered software, making business applications more intuitive.
* The acquisition aimed to streamline user onboarding, reduce software learning curves, and improve productivity.

### AMD Took Over ZT Systems for $4.9 Billion

AMD strategically pushed into cloud computing infrastructure [by acquiring ZT Systems for $4.9 billion](https://www.wsj.com/tech/ai/amd-deal-shows-ai-chip-business-isnt-just-about-chips-81fb46d9). This move helped AMD expand its data center capabilities and strengthen competition with Intel and Nvidia.

* ZT Systems is a key supplier of server solutions for hyperscale cloud providers and enterprise data centers.
* The acquisition allowed AMD to scale its high-performance computing (HPC) and AI-driven data center offerings.
* AMD leveraged ZT Systems’ expertise to improve cloud workload performance and efficiency.
* This deal positioned AMD to compete more aggressively in AI, machine learning, and cloud computing markets.

### ThoughtWorks Acquired by Apax Partners for $1.7 Billion

ThoughtWorks, a global technology consultancy, was acquired by private equity firm Apax Partners for $1.7 billion. This acquisition took ThoughtWorks private, allowing for strategic expansion under Apax’s leadership.

* ThoughtWorks specializes in software development, cloud solutions, and enterprise digital transformation.
* Apax Partners, a private equity firm, focused on scaling ThoughtWorks’ AI and cloud-based service offerings.
* The acquisition enabled ThoughtWorks to expand its global presence and deepen partnerships with AWS and Google Cloud.
* Under private ownership, ThoughtWorks aimed to accelerate innovation and improve enterprise technology solutions.

### Nvidia Acquired Run:AI for $700 Million

Nvidia strengthened its AI infrastructure capabilities [by acquiring Run:AI for $700 million](https://www.reuters.com/markets/deals/nvidia-closes-700-mln-runai-acquisition-after-regulatory-hurdles-2024-12-30/). This acquisition enabled Nvidia to optimize AI workload orchestration and expand its AI data center management dominance.

* Run:AI specializes in AI workload orchestration, allowing companies to optimize GPU usage for machine learning and deep learning applications.
* Nvidia aimed to integrate Run:AI’s solutions into its AI-driven cloud and data center operations.
* The deal allowed Nvidia to improve the efficiency of AI model training and deployment across cloud environments.
* By acquiring Run:AI, Nvidia expanded its influence in AI research, enterprise AI adoption, and high-performance computing.

* The deal allowed Salesforce to regain control over a critical segment of its customer relationship management (CRM) portfolio.
* The acquisition aligned with Salesforce’s strategy of consolidating AI-driven business automation within its ecosystem.
* Salesforce aimed to enhance its AI-powered analytics, sales automation, and customer service tools.
* The move strengthened Salesforce’s ability to deliver seamless enterprise solutions while maintaining product innovation.

### Google Invested $2.7 Billion in Character.AI

This investment bolstered Google’s Gemini initiative and accelerated the development of advanced AI chatbots and virtual assistants.

* Character.AI is an AI-driven platform focused on personalized chatbot interactions and conversational AI models.
* Google’s investment supported Character.AI’s expansion into enterprise applications, virtual assistants, and creative AI tools.
* The funding helped Google integrate Character.AI’s capabilities into its Gemini AI ecosystem, enhancing AI-driven user interactions.
* Google aimed to compete with OpenAI and Anthropic by leveraging Character.AI’s conversational AI expertise.

### Thoma Bravo Took Darktrace for $5.3 Billion

* Darktrace is a UK-based cybersecurity company specializing in AI-driven threat detection and response.
* Thoma Bravo sought to integrate Darktrace’s AI-powered security tools into its existing cybersecurity investments.
* The acquisition strengthened Thoma Bravo’s portfolio of security-focused companies, enhancing its presence in enterprise cybersecurity.
* Darktrace continued to operate independently while leveraging Thoma Bravo’s financial backing for global expansion.

### Veeam Invested $21 Million in Alcion

Veeam, a leader in data backup and disaster recovery solutions, invested $21 million in Series A funding for Alcion. This investment aimed to enhance cloud-based data protection and ransomware recovery capabilities.

* Alcion develops next-generation backup and cybersecurity solutions, focusing on protecting cloud workloads from ransomware threats.
* Veeam’s investment enabled Alcion to scale its operations and accelerate innovation in AI-powered data protection.
* The partnership positioned Veeam as a leader in AI-driven backup and disaster recovery solutions.
* Alcion’s technology was integrated into Veeam’s cloud backup platform, improving ransomware detection and mitigation.

### Wiz Acquired Cloud Remediation Startup Dazz for $450 Million

* The acquisition allowed Wiz to offer more advanced security automation tools for enterprises managing multi-cloud environments.
* Wiz strengthened its position as a leading cloud security and vulnerability management provider.

# Humans only

Glassdoor has been built on the contributions of real employees and job seekers. We use advanced security systems to keep our site safe and prevent misuse or unauthorized access.

In rare cases, security protections may mistakenly block legitimate activity from real users. If you have been mistakenly blocked from accessing our site, please review our [Help Center article](https://help.glassdoor.com/s/article/Troubleshooting-Tips?language=en_US) for troubleshooting steps.

# Réservé aux humains

Glassdoor est fondé sur les contributions de véritables employés et chercheurs d’emploi. Nous utilisons des systèmes de sécurité sophistiqués pour assurer la sécurité de notre site et empêcher toute utilisation abusive ou tout accès non autorisé.

Dans de rares cas, ces protections de sécurité peuvent bloquer par erreur les activités légitimes d’utilisateurs réels. Si votre accès à notre site a été bloqué par erreur, veuillez consulter l’[article de notre centre d’aide](https://aide.glassdoor.fr/s/article/Astuces-de-depannage?language=fr) pour prendre connaissance des étapes de dépannage.

Glassdoor wurde auf den Beiträgen echter Mitarbeiter:innen und Stellensuchenden aufgebaut. Wir verwenden fortschrittliche Sicherheitssysteme, um unsere Seite sicher zu halten und Missbrauch oder unbefugten Zugriff zu verhindern.

Falls Ihr Zugriff auf unsere Seite versehentlich gesperrt wurde, lesen Sie bitte unseren [Artikel im Hilfebereich](https://hilfe.glassdoor.de/s/article/Tipps-zur-Fehlerbehebung?language=de) mit Schritten zur Fehlerbehebung.

# Alleen voor mensen

Glassdoor vertrouwt op de bijdragen van echte werknemers en werkzoekenden. We gebruiken geavanceerde beveiligingssystemen om onze site veilig te houden en misbruik of ongeautoriseerde toegang te voorkomen.

In zeldzame gevallen kunnen beveiligingsmaatregelen onbedoeld legitieme activiteiten van echte gebruikers blokkeren. Als je onverwacht geen toegang krijgt tot onze site, bekijk dan ons [Helpcenter-artikel](https://help.glassdoor.nl/s/article/Tips-voor-het-oplossen-van-problemen?language=nl_NL) voor stappen om het probleem op te lossen.

tuo accesso al nostro sito è stato bloccato per errore, puoi
cercare la soluzione nel nostro
[articolo del Centro assistenza](https://aiuto.glassdoor.it/s/article/Suggerimenti-per-la-risoluzione-dei-problemi?language=it).

## Overview

With a decade of experience, Capsitech is a dedicated software development firm with offices in the UK and India. The company focuses exclusively on development, transforming client concepts into high-quality, custom digital products. Their core service is building powerful and scalable web and mobile applications, delivering tailor-made software solutions that drive business value for their clients.

Title: Cloud Healthcare API Services | Secure Data Integration & Analytics
# Cloud Healthcare API Integration Services

What We Do?

## Enhance Patient Care with Cloud Healthcare API Integration Services

Cloud-based solutions are becoming important in the healthcare business for improving patient care, enhancing operations, easy access to healthcare data, connecting various healthcare systems, allowing actual time data exchange, and boosting collaboration across healthcare providers. By utilizing these integrations, healthcare providers can manage patient’s personal information, encourage telemedical services, and follow industry rules regulations.

At APITech, we specialize in Cloud Healthcare API Integration services that upgrade healthcare operations by allowing systematic data reconciliation and system integration. Our expert team works with healthcare providers to design customized API solutions that smoothly connect various cloud-based platforms such as EHR/EMR systems, patient management tools, and telemedicine software whether you need to integrate cloud healthcare integration solution with your existing infrastructure or develop new ones.

Partner with [APITech](https://www.apiintegrationtech.com/) for Cloud Healthcare API Integration services and upgrade your patient care!

[Let's Build Your API](/contact-us)

## Cloud healthcare API Integration services we offer

We deliver complete cloud healthcare API integration services designed to modernize healthcare operations, enhance patient care, and improve data accessibility. Below are the key services we offer:

* **Cerner API Integration :**Cerner API Integration Services allow smooth data exchange, improve patient care, and simplify clinical workflows. [Cerner API](https://www.healthmeasures.net/implement-healthmeasures/administration-platforms/cerner) boosts real-time access to patient information for efficient management and compliance.
* **Epic API Integration:**[Epic API](https://open.epic.com/) simplifies the connection between Epic’s electronic health record systems and other healthcare applications. Epic API Integration services simplify patient data sharing for improved clinical workflows.
* **Allscripts API Integration:**Our Allscripts API Integration Services provide powerful data management solutions, improving healthcare delivery. [Allscripts API](https://developer.allscripts.com/FHIR?PageTitle=GetStarted) allows smooth integration for efficient patient records management across various systems.

* **Athenahealth API Integration:**Athenahealth API Integration Services simplify patient data management, improving appointment scheduling and reducing administrative workload.  [Athenahealth API](https://www.athenahealth.com/developer-portal) integrates important features for better patient engagement and treatment outcomes.
* **GE Healthcare API Integration**[GE Healthcare API](https://logon.gehealthcare.com/GEIDPLoginPage?startURL=%2Fsetup%2Fsecur%2FRemoteAccessAuthorizationPage.apexp%3Fsource%3DCAAAAZQvvWY5MDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwAAAA_A2YTruK1Ro8FRoPVfAAJIZlO3oFMQLgG53z3CikBuQgiYHl2oIhgzW_6FzS3c1Uz9WLBnG-iZ-TG21_VQMdc_IMmThBJO-UdNfSS5dg5jHMzPuoS5OIEKC3uRWQYKOGPTRQ6Dh_CLtlmYnK4cgh6Ls40b71lOFA7oXto4TzD_PtcqIli8lsNrOQ2az2_y7tJPHEehlcIof2nOlDbBbke6Cm0zTAyZvz1SIKOi9jeURYkNplXtDtai78wVkm6sP9v11uQRDiy2k_jHMS1W1xGlzEOHYa7qa795THlSdwCKWYFW8OBY8V7QibkUDH3tNMINfaUa8ZzkMxOypE2TQ253xxzHSHQdcRhKVgii-kHlhoaXp0tw5aEpxYzaaetGPeYSsxxO30nj2p7ASuZzjcAHd8y1Um9nDEG1shSwp885WmMvwa5kqw9vKwm9VaVOM3dHwYHUUhAIJjOYzlY5lubKR5shbP_tfLD_4Q45S2t8POa4ODcjYPoXYW01iRvN_w-JeLMX_cRpKuAX_VmadZWqISN28ugsdPo12TtyAiiV3XAxphsXlbMO1hU356CYC81Nc_bZYSyZEpWQqJxWX8msAJoFLuzJCzhOscsIXnWQLqCh_3cqZPYWL2fipDfUt09dULeSM48IjWDLZZ59lZFW1VACwl1w28tZOOssaiwAcaqKO0OK9x1J9n5Et99C_aJn0oGPVT6CStXSjwhH3KsqGdwP1VB31e2pOL4ezEwD5nRGH0AjhkXOZPnOFbHtb1UEWhxxPW9c4ICzfo39ZwEKZ0mjUD6lik0EugSbfSCMK1wRKeYTXBq19CvzkqQuMs_DaLqdthiVDm0bKgOLua6OFB3dgcOKf81OYPwmhEvN7NI99gRy6pGmG6NckHkQq8nng5_843kEmgZw3LBW64ZjRSzPtRhzI42iuAvPkEqCQduxL5NoUitXBbgblXMLWxS_u2A00TXIeEPbBHE6sZfiB3NDvvXMZBG49E4fQnropw&login_hint=app%3D0sp0c000000PBAg%26sourceURL%3Dwww.gehealthcare.com%26username%3Ddefault%40ge.com%26language%3Den&sdtd=1) improves imaging and diagnostics data management, ensuring better patient care and workflow efficiency. GE Healthcare API Integration Services allows smooth integration with hospital management systems.
* **Meditech API Integration**APITech’s Meditech API Integration Services upgrade patient management and improve clinical decision-making. [Meditech API](https://home.meditech.com/en/d/restapiresources/pages/apidoc.htm) provides smooth interoperability for patient record access and management.

* **Teladoc Health API Integration:**  [Teladoc Health API](https://www.teladochealth.com/) enhances virtual care management. Teladoc Health API Integration Services allows healthcare providers to provide secure, authentic telemedicine services, and improve convenience for patients.
* **Amwell API Integration:**Amwell API Integration Services improve virtual care platforms, allowing secure communication between healthcare professionals and patients.  [Amwell API](https://code.amwell.com/apis) provides a smooth telemedicine experience.
* **Zoom Healthcare API Integration:**Our Zoom Healthcare API Integration Services allow telehealth communication and collaboration for improved patient care. [Zoom Healthcare API](https://devforum.zoom.us/t/integrating-zoom-api-in-healthcare-software-opportunities-and-challenges/110159) integrates video conferencing and collaboration tools to simplify virtual visits.

* **DICOM API Integration:**DICOM API Integration Services simplify the sharing and viewing of medical images. [DICOM API](https://cloud.google.com/healthcare-api/docs/concepts/dicom) ensures interaction between imaging devices and healthcare systems for improved diagnosis and treatment planning.
* **PACS System API Integration:**[PACS System API](https://cloud.google.com/healthcare-api/docs/how-tos/dicom-connect-pacs) provides smooth access to digital imaging data, improving workflow and collaboration. PACS System API Integration Services integrates various imaging modalities for easy recovery and storage of patient images.

* **Google Cloud Healthcare API Integration:**Our Google Cloud Healthcare API Integration Services improve health data analysis, providing valuable insights. [Google Cloud Healthcare API](https://cloud.google.com/healthcare-api?hl=en) provides efficient data processing and improved decision-making for better patient outcomes.
* **Microsoft Azure Healthcare API Integration:**Microsoft Azure Healthcare API Integration Services allow healthcare organizations to analyze large datasets efficiently. Microsoft Azure Healthcare API provides scalable solutions for health data management and analytics.
* **AWS HealthLake API Integration:**[AWS HealthLake API](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/healthlake/)  simplifies the management and analysis of health data, allowing for enhanced patient care and faster treatment decisions. This popular meme is humorous—but it also highlights a serious engineering principle: 👉 Syntax alone does not define a programming language. Context does. JavaScript may allow C++-like expressions (such as ++), but that doesn’t make it C++. Languages are defined by their execution model, runtime behavior, memory management, and design philosophy: not by shared symbols. In software engineering, being technically correct without being precise can be misleading. And in real-world systems: • Small misconceptions can snowball into poor design decisions • Vague explanations can cause major technical confusion • Precision in communication is just as important as precision in code 💡 𝗧𝗵𝗲 𝘁𝗮𝗸𝗲𝗮𝘄𝗮𝘆: Good engineers don’t just write correct code, they communicate ideas clearly and accurately. It should be robust enough to anchor mission-critical operations, yet seamless enough to disappear into the background of your daily success. It shouldn't be a hurdle your team has to clear—it should be the main support. # Capsitech IT Interview Experience for Full Stack Developer Role (On-Campus)

Last Updated : 3 Apr, 2025

Hello Everyone! I am a candidate from Jodhpur, Rajasthan, who has been selected for a Full Stack Developer role with Capsitech. The interview process was conducted in multiple rounds, and I’m happy to share my journey and insights as I look forward to starting my career with the company.

### ****Recruitment Process Overview****

* Round 1: MCQ Round
* Round 2: Technical Interview 1
* Round 3: Technical Interview 2
* Round 4: HR Round

### ****Round 1: MCQ Round****

* ****Date:**** 23rd October 2024
* ****Duration:**** 30 minutes
* ****Method:**** Online test
* ****Focus:**** Basic technical MCQs

#### ****Key Areas from where MCQs is asked:****

* HTML, CSS, JavaScript fundamentals
* General web development concepts

#### ****Tips:****

* Solve MCQs as quickly and accurately as possible
* Focus on fundamental concepts in HTML, CSS, and JavaScript
* Use platforms like InterviewBit for practice

****Obstacles:**** Time management, maintaining accuracy

****Outcome:**** Cleared the round and moved on to the next round.

### ****Round 2: Technical Interview 1****

* ****Date:**** 13th November 2024
* ****Duration:**** 15-20 minutes
* ****Method:**** Online
* ****Focus:**** Frontend and Backend Development Basic Easy Concepts

#### ****Key Areas:****

* HTML & CSS basics
* JavaScript (let, var, const, functions, async/await)
* React.js (Components, Hooks, Counter app using useState)
* Object-Oriented Programming (Classes, Objects, Inheritance, Polymorphism, Encapsulation)
* SQL simple queries
* Basic Data Structures and Algorithms (Arrays, Strings, Numbers)

#### ****Preparation Material:****

* YouTube tutorials, ChatGPT for quick explanations
* Search for "HTML Top Interview Questions"

****Obstacles:**** Depth of understanding in JavaScript and React.js

****Outcome:**** Cleared the round and received an invitation for Round 3.

### ****Round 3: Technical Interview 2****

* ****Date:**** 23rd November 2024
* ****Duration:**** 20-30 minutes
* ****Method:**** Online
* ****Focus:**** Advanced technical knowledge & problem-solving

****Key Questions:****

* Data Structures and Algorithms (Topics - ****Arrays, Strings, Linked Lists, Matrices, Stacks****)
* DSA Question: Given an array of subarrays where each inner array contains 1, 2, or 3 elements, multiply the elements inside each inner array and then sum up the results.
* React.js (****Advanced Hooks, Components, State Management****)
* Node.js, Express.js (****Async/Await, HTTP Requests, Middleware****)
* API handling (****Aggregation, Lookup, Authentication vs Authorization****)
* Code Implementation: Fetching an API within 3 seconds

****Preparation Material:****

* GFG Top 150 DSA questions
* React.js documentation and advanced concepts
* Node.js and Express.js interview questions
* Revise OOP principles and important keywords

****Obstacles:**** Implementing efficient solutions under time constraints

****Outcome:**** Cleared the round and moved on to the final HR round.

### Round 4: HR Round

* ****Date:**** 15th December 2024
* ****Duration:**** 5-10 Minutes
* ****Method:**** In-person (in college campus )
* ****Focus:**** General HR discussions

#### ****Key Questions:****

* Self-introduction
* Willingness to relocate
* Family background and support
* Familiarity with the company and its projects
* Famous place in your hometown

#### ****Pro Tips:****

* Be confident and natural
* Avoid over-preparing responses
* Research about Capsitech’s projects if time permits

****Obstacles:**** None (HR round is informal and casual)

****Outcome:**** Successfully cleared the HR round.

### ****Final Outcome****

I am pleased to share that I have been ****SELECTED**** for the Full Stack Developer role with Capsitech, with an offered salary of ****6 LPA****. The result was communicated on ****18th December 2024****, and I have received the ****Letter of Intent (LOI)****.

Overall, the interview experience was structured and fair, effectively testing the fundamental skills required for the role. I’m excited about the opportunity to join Capsitech and look forward to the next steps in my journey with the company.

Comment

# Top API Integration Tools in 2026

This article breaks down API integration tools, from iPaaS to unified APIs and marketplaces, showing how they save months of development, cut complexity, and help companies scale faster. With real-world examples, it’s a clear guide to choosing the right tool for your business growth.

## What is an API Integration Tool?

API integration tools connect different software applications, enabling them to share data and functionality without manual intervention. These tools range from visual workflow builders that non-technical users can operate to developer-focused platforms that provide unified endpoints for accessing multiple services. They handle the complex technical requirements of API connections, such as authentication, data transformation, error handling, rate limiting, and monitoring so that teams can focus on business logic rather than integration plumbing.

Modern API integration tools fall into several categories. Some provide drag-and-drop interfaces for creating workflows between applications. Others offer single API endpoints that connect to dozens of similar services. Enterprise-grade solutions add governance, security, and scalability features for managing hundreds of APIs across large organizations.

## Why Do You Need One?

Building and maintaining API integrations in-house consumes significant engineering resources. Each integration requires understanding provider-specific documentation, handling authentication methods, managing data transformations, and maintaining compatibility as APIs evolve. A single integration can take weeks to build and requires ongoing maintenance as providers update their APIs.

The average SaaS application today connects to 15-20 other services. Enterprise companies often manage hundreds of integrations across departments. Without proper tooling, this creates an integration backlog that blocks product development and frustrates customers who expect seamless connectivity.

API integration tools solve these problems by abstracting complexity, providing pre-built connectors, and handling infrastructure concerns. They reduce integration development time from months to days or even hours. They also centralize monitoring, error handling, and compliance, which is critical for maintaining reliable integrations at scale.

For SaaS companies specifically, offering robust integrations directly impacts revenue. Customers increasingly choose products based on ecosystem connectivity. The faster you can add integrations, the more deals you win. API integration tools make this speed possible without proportionally scaling engineering teams.

## iPaaS (Integration Platform as a Service)

[iPaaS](https://www.apideck.com/blog/differences-between-embedded-ipaas-and-unified-apis-saas-integrations) platforms connect SaaS applications through visual workflows and pre-built connectors. They're designed for teams that need integration without heavy engineering investment.

### Zapier

[Zapier](https://www.apideck.com/blog/unified-api-vs-zapier) democratized automation by making it accessible to non-technical users through its intuitive interface and massive app ecosystem. With over 6,000 pre-built connectors, it handles simple point-to-point integrations and complex multi-step workflows equally well. The platform's strength lies in its simplicity. Users can create "Zaps" that trigger actions across multiple applications without writing code. While it excels at business automation and rapid prototyping, limitations emerge at scale with restricted customization options, no support for complex data transformations, and pricing that escalates quickly with task volume.

**Common use cases:**

* Marketing teams automating lead flow from Typeform → HubSpot → Slack notifications
* Sales teams syncing new deals from CRM to project management tools
* Support teams creating tickets from emails and form submissions
* Content teams publishing across multiple platforms simultaneously

### MuleSoft Anypoint Platform

Salesforce's MuleSoft represents the enterprise end of the iPaaS spectrum, built on an API-led connectivity approach that treats every integration as a reusable asset. The platform combines design, development, and management capabilities in a unified environment that handles both cloud and on-premise systems. It provides enterprise-grade features like distributed transaction management, complex error handling, and comprehensive monitoring across hybrid deployments. MuleSoft's DataWeave transformation language enables sophisticated data mapping between systems with different schemas. The platform requires significant investment in training and infrastructure but delivers unmatched capability for large-scale enterprise integration scenarios.

**Common use cases:**

* Banks integrating legacy on-premise systems with modern cloud applications
* Healthcare organizations syncing patient data across EHR systems while maintaining HIPAA compliance
* Retail chains connecting POS systems, inventory management, and e-commerce platforms
* Manufacturing companies orchestrating supply chain data across partners

### Boomi

Dell Boomi balances enterprise capabilities with user accessibility through its AtomSphere platform, which provides both low-code development and advanced customization options. The platform's distributed architecture uses lightweight "Atoms" that can be deployed anywhere—cloud, on-premise, or edge—enabling true hybrid integration. Boomi's extensive connector library covers most enterprise applications, and its Master Data Hub provides data quality and governance features often missing in other iPaaS solutions. The platform particularly excels at B2B/EDI integration scenarios with built-in trading partner management. Real-time and batch processing capabilities handle varying integration patterns, though the platform's full potential requires technical expertise to unlock.

**Common use cases:**

* Logistics companies synchronizing ERP, CRM, and EDI transactions across trading partners
* E-commerce businesses connecting Shopify/Magento with warehouse management systems
* Financial services integrating core banking with customer portals
* SaaS companies building multi-tenant integration infrastructure

### Workato

Workato positions itself as the integration platform for both IT and business users, offering enterprise-grade capabilities through an accessible interface. The platform's "recipe" approach combines pre-built integration templates with customization options, allowing teams to start fast and iterate as needed. Workato's intelligent automation includes machine learning features for data mapping suggestions and anomaly detection. The platform handles complex scenarios like long-running workflows, conditional logic, and error recovery without requiring deep technical knowledge. Its enterprise features include private cloud deployment options, advanced security controls, and comprehensive audit logging. The recipe marketplace accelerates deployment, though costs can surprise teams used to simpler tools.

**Common use cases:**

* HR departments automating employee onboarding across Workday, Slack, Okta, and IT systems
* Finance teams synchronizing data between NetSuite, Salesforce, and reporting tools
* IT teams orchestrating ticket routing between ServiceNow, Jira, and Slack
* Revenue operations connecting CPQ, billing, and revenue recognition systems

### SnapLogic

SnapLogic's Intelligent Integration Platform combines traditional iPaaS capabilities with AI-powered automation through its IRIS (Integration Assistant) technology. The platform uses machine learning to suggest data mappings, predict integration patterns, and recommend optimizations based on usage patterns across its customer base. SnapLogic's pipeline architecture processes both streaming and batch data, making it suitable for real-time integration and large-scale data migration projects. The platform provides over 700 pre-built "Snaps" (connectors) and supports custom development for proprietary systems. Its self-service capabilities reduce IT bottlenecks while maintaining governance through centralized monitoring and control.

**Common use cases:**

* Analytics platforms aggregating data from multiple sources into unified dashboards
* Retail companies syncing inventory across channels in real-time
* Healthcare providers consolidating patient data from multiple systems
* Financial institutions building data lakes from disparate sources

### Celigo

Celigo focuses on the intersection of business applications and data integration, particularly excelling at ERP-centric scenarios. The platform provides Integration Apps—pre-built, yet customizable integration templates that encapsulate best practices for common integration patterns. These templates reduce implementation time by up to 80% compared to building from scratch. Celigo's SmartConnectors handle the nuances of complex applications like NetSuite, Salesforce, and Shopify, managing API limits, bulk operations, and error recovery automatically. While more limited in scope than general-purpose iPaaS platforms, Celigo's specialized approach delivers faster time-to-value for supported use cases.

**Common use cases:**

* Shopify merchants syncing orders, customers, and inventory with NetSuite ERP
* Amazon sellers managing multi-channel inventory and fulfillment
* B2B companies automating order-to-cash processes
* Subscription businesses connecting billing with accounting systems

### Cyclr

Cyclr takes a unique embedded approach to iPaaS, designed specifically for SaaS vendors who want to offer native integrations without building infrastructure. The platform provides white-label integration capabilities that can be embedded directly into SaaS applications, maintaining consistent branding and user experience. Cyclr handles the technical complexity of API connections while giving SaaS vendors control over which integrations to expose and how users interact with them. The platform includes a marketplace framework for managing and monetizing integrations, along with analytics to understand usage patterns. Its lightweight architecture minimizes performance impact o

- **Furniture sourcing involves the process of procuring raw materials, components, and finished products to manufacture or sell furniture. Ensuring ethical practices in furniture sourcing is crucial to address environmental, social, and economic considerations. Here's a detailed overview: 1. Material Selection: Wood Sourcing: Prioritize responsibly sourced wood from certified forests. The FSC certification ensures sustainable forestry practices. Alternative Materials: Explore the use of alternative materials such as bamboo, recycled metal, or reclaimed wood to reduce environmental impact. 2. Supplier Vetting: Ethical Labor Practices: Choose suppliers that adhere to fair labor standards. Regularly assess suppliers through audits to ensure compliance with ethical labor practices. Transparency: Seek suppliers who are transparent about their sourcing practices and provide detailed information about the origins of materials. 3. Local and Global Sourcing: Local Sourcing: Consider sourcing materials locally to support regional economies and reduce the carbon footprint associated with transportation. Global Partnerships: Explore global partnerships for specialized materials, ensuring that suppliers align with ethical and sustainable standards. 4. Environmental Impact: Eco-friendly Processes: Select manufacturers that employ environmentally friendly production processes, minimizing waste and energy consumption. Product Lifecycle: Consider the entire lifecycle of furniture, including its end-of-life impact. Design products that are recyclable or biodegradable. 5. Certifications: ISO Certification: Look for suppliers with ISO certifications, such as ISO 14001 for environmental management systems, FSC for sustainable wood used in manufacturing, VRIKSH for legal origin of wood as indicators of commitment to sustainable practices. 6. Social Responsibility: Community Engagement: Support suppliers who engage positively with the communities where they operate. This may include contributing to local development projects or promoting social welfare initiatives. Inclusivity: Encourage suppliers to embrace diversity and inclusivity within their workforce. 7. Continuous Improvement: Regular Audits: Conduct regular audits to assess and improve sourcing practices, ensuring ongoing compliance with ethical standards. Adaptation to Change: Stay informed about evolving industry standards and global best practices, adapting sourcing strategies accordingly. By integrating these elements into furniture sourcing practices, businesses can contribute to a more ethical and sustainable industry while meeting the growing demand for environmentally conscious products. #furnituresolutions #globalsourcing #furnitureindustry #sourcingandprocurement #sourcingstrategy #sourcingspecialist #sustainability #furnitures #globalsourcing #ecommercebusiness #furnituredesign #ethicalsourcing #globalbusiness**

# Ashish Yadav: Biography and Career

Ashish Yadav provides his contact information and educational and professional qualifications. He has an M.E. in Production from SGSITS Indore with 7.84% and a B.E. in Mechanical from MITS Gwalior with 68.43%. His experience includes working as an Assistant Professor at various institutions in Indore and Gwalior from 2010 to 2014. Additional personal details provided include his name, parents' names, date of birth, hobbies, languages known, father's occupation, and annual salary.

Title: Ashish Yadav Curriculum Vitae | DOC
# Ashish Yadav Curriculum Vitae

Ashish .C. Yadav has over 5 years of experience in billing and cash management roles for the ATM industry. He is currently a MIS Executive at Diebold Systems handling billing processes, accounts receivable, and revenue tracking. Previously he held roles at Tata Communications and Scientific Security Management Services involving billing, cash replenishment, and coordination with banks and vendors. Yadav has a Bachelor's degree in Commerce and is pursuing an MBA in Finance. His skills include Oracle, SAP, Excel, and communication.

![Google Drive](/images/next/svg/google-drive.svg?v=257210806e8bff4d0d4d6e4f609fe2d6fdf2f92a)
![ASHISH .C. YADAV
SKILLS & EXPERTISE:
• Managing end to end support of ATM installations.
• Managing lifecycle of ATM’s in coordination with banks.
• Understanding the VOC of customers & putting it across the management
for process corrections.
• Driving partner to deliver the agreed deliverables with the desired quality
laid by the organization.
• Setting targets for monthly collection & working closely with team to
achieve the set targets.
• Leading a team handling Documentation, Billing & Back office Operations
for collections.
PROFESSIONAL EXPERIENCE:
Organization: Diebold Systems Private Limited.
Designation: MIS Executive – Billing/Credit Control
Since: 23rd
Feb 2016 till date.
ROLE & RESPONSIBILITIES:
ATM Service Team (Billing Process), Using Tool Oracle:
 Daily follow up for payment and MIS preparation for
Accounts Receivable West Region
 Tracking the ATM & other product from delivery till
revenue for West Region
 Collection of ICs (Installation Certificate)
 Maintaining Collection Report & Submitting
Payment receipt advice to Finance.
 Verifying & Submission of assets Bills to Customers.
 MIS report on Invoice & submission.
 Follow up with territory managers for timely
submission of invoice sets.
 Verifying & Submission of Consumable Invoices
to Internal Customers.

### 

"Our patients want innovative solutions!" Actually… your patients want to book appointments without friction.
Healthcare providers often invest in:
❌ Custom telehealth platforms with low adoption
❌ Branded apps that patients never download
❌ Patient portals that require training to use
In India, the biggest health apps ever built reached a maximum of 5 million users. WhatsApp reaches 850 million users. That's a 170x difference in reach.
Here’s what actually drives return:
✅ Appointment booking that takes under 60 seconds
✅ Automated reminders that reduce no-shows by 40%+
✅ Lab results delivered instantly through Whatsapp
✅ Patient questions answered without overwhelming front desk
I've seen clinics launch custom apps with every feature imaginable and end up with a 15% adoption rate across their existing patient base.
Same clinic adds WhatsApp booking and within one week, over 60% of appointments come through a platform patients already check multiple times a day.
This is what operational efficiency looks like.
One solution required you to change patient behavior AND train your staff. The other automated repetitive tasks and met patients where they already were.
You’re not "settling for less innovation.” Innovation removes friction so well, you forget the technology is even there.

Everyone is acting like it’s 2014 again. 🦖
I see agencies still fighting over "Keyword Density" and stuffing articles with phrases like "Best Digital Agency in Pune" 50 times.
Meanwhile, your customers are just asking ChatGPT: "Hey, who can actually build me a good app without ripping me off?"
And the AI isn't counting your keywords. It’s reading your intent.
We are entering the era of Answer Engine Optimization (AEO), but half the industry is still trying to trick a Google algorithm that doesn't exist anymore.
Stop writing for robots that died 5 years ago. Start writing for humans (and the smart robots that read like humans).
At FurOnLabs, we focus on Problem Solving, not Keyword Stuffing. Because frankly, even the AI is tired of reading your "SEO Optimized" fluff. 😂
